  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_0d11f56b-e67c-48cd-88c6-a377edb16f2e'
      });

<div id="descriptionContainer">
  
      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer8316032683066465583">Dewi Lestari yang bernama pena Dee, kali ini hadir dengan mahakarya unik dan pertama di Indonesia. "Rectoverso" merupakan hibrida dari fiksi dan musik, terdiri dari sebelas cerita pendek dan sebelas lagu yang bisa dinikmati secara terpisah maupun bersama-sama. Keduanya saling melengkapi bagaikan dua imaji yang seolah berdiri sendiri tapi sesungguhnya merupakan satu kesatua</span>
  <span id="freeText8316032683066465583" style="display:none">Dewi Lestari yang bernama pena Dee, kali ini hadir dengan mahakarya unik dan pertama di Indonesia. "Rectoverso" merupakan hibrida dari fiksi dan musik, terdiri dari sebelas cerita pendek dan sebelas lagu yang bisa dinikmati secara terpisah maupun bersama-sama. Keduanya saling melengkapi bagaikan dua imaji yang seolah berdiri sendiri tapi sesungguhnya merupakan satu kesatuan. Inilah cermin dari dua dunia Dewi Lestari yang ia ekspresikan dalam napas kreatifitas tunggal bertajuk "Rectoverso". Dengar fiksinya. Baca musiknya. Lengkapi penghayatan anda dan temukanlah sebuah pengalaman baru.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer15076569280267298681">i was lucky to get this book in a complete package with the cd directly from the rectoverso marketing team (dewi signed them, thanks dee). will explain later why i'm only giving three stars to a book written by my favorite author ;)<br/><br/>okay, so here it is. i first fell in love with her writing through supernova 1 (which i've read probably more than 10 times, cover-to-cover), i thought and still think that it's the most brilliantly written fiction book in indonesia so far: it's sad but not sappy, sma</span>
  <span id="freeText15076569280267298681" style="display:none">i was lucky to get this book in a complete package with the cd directly from the rectoverso marketing team (dewi signed them, thanks dee). will explain later why i'm only giving three stars to a book written by my favorite author ;)<br /><br />okay, so here it is. i first fell in love with her writing through supernova 1 (which i've read probably more than 10 times, cover-to-cover), i thought and still think that it's the most brilliantly written fiction book in indonesia so far: it's sad but not sappy, smart without trying too hard, deep without saying it bluntly that it's deep, even covertly mischievous at some parts . then i found supernova 2 (which i've read only once), and then supernova 3 (which is very different from supernova 1, but i still can't enjoy it thoroughly to read twice).<br /><br />i have never - however - read any of her short stories, including filosofi kopi. when rectoverso arrived at my desk, the 1st thing that i did was sync the whole cd to my ipod and spent the rest of the working day listening to it, and i love it! andy rianto's arrangement is impressive. it took me another two weeks, though, to finally find the time to read the book. you see, i love dee's words: they're everything that any writer should do - tell a story like it is but tell it like you're telling the most important story to the readers. and i guess i'm just not that big a fan of short stories, just when i started to enjoy her paragraphs, it jerks me away from the storyline with an abrupt ending. maybe it's the fault of my mindset of entering the reading experience like i was gonna read a whole novel.<br /><br />nevertheless, the book was a great reading, invaluable at some parts, and definitely push me into an even more extreme hunger of her next work (any idea when perahu kertas is available on printed edition?).<br /><br />my favorite chapters (and if i were her, i would write a whole book to continue these): <br />Peluk, Grow A Day Older (my number 1 favorite!), and Tidur.</span>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText14401660313330842142" style="display:none">Interesting. I haven't listened to the album (yet) but I have this feeling that it's gonna be as awesome (if not more) as the book.<br /><br />11 little stories, accentuated with cute little graphics that somehow reminds me of Tim Burton, which are mysterious and touching and beautiful all at the same time. "This has been nothing but a cosmic joke, ha-ha, very funny, and will you please excuse me now?". Great. Cheesy, but great.<br /><br />And the ones with the kid eating the back of a chicken, and how Dee compares it to love. Ah, I would try to translate it to English, but it would lose half its meaning. <div id="review_36354926" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

<span id="freeTextContainer624282197638060406">I don’t know how to describe this book, except for the obvious that this book contains of 11 independent stories, which although didn’t relate with each other but somehow connected by invisible silver line. <br/><br/>About how the story is written, it’s just Dee being herself.   <span id="freeText624282197638060406" style="display:none">I don’t know how to describe this book, except for the obvious that this book contains of 11 independent stories, which although didn’t relate with each other but somehow connected by invisible silver line. <br /><br />About how the story is written, it’s just Dee being herself. It’s good, brilliantly written, I love how she choose her words and her description of places and feelings. It doesn’t need too much conversation between the characters to liven up the book, descriptions of emotions and places are enough. <br /><br />Most of the stories will make you think, about the story, the characters and yourself. I found similarities, both in characters and situation, with myself, so I enjoyed this book very much. This book was a gift, from a dear friend, too bad he didn’t include the CD :P so I couldn’t tell much about the hybrid experience this book was intended to be, a mixture of reading and listening to the soundtracks at the same time. The book is good though, makes me wonder how this book would feel if I listened to the music too….<br /><br /></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer708002215" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13239497180819679532">This is the first romance novel which didn't make me cringe while reading all the stories. <br/><br/>All eleven stories represent a real situation you'd find in real life, or you never thought you'd find in the real life but it's there.<br/>I personally don't like Indonesian romance books in general, only some could fit my taste, but I feel love, I fall in love in reality so I can enjoy this as much. :)<br/><br/>I always love how Dee makes each sentences, each song lyrics. I've heard some songs before reading the story </span>
  <span id="freeText13239497180819679532" style="display:none">This is the first romance novel which didn't make me cringe while reading all the stories. <br /><br />All eleven stories represent a real situation you'd find in real life, or you never thought you'd find in the real life but it's there.<br />I personally don't like Indonesian romance books in general, only some could fit my taste, but I feel love, I fall in love in reality so I can enjoy this as much. :)<br /><br />I always love how Dee makes each sentences, each song lyrics. I've heard some songs before reading the story and I was like 'Oh so this is what the song means.' The 2 English stories are also enjoyable. I almost doubted Dee's talent to write as beautiful in English, but she's proven me wrong. Her English words are beautiful too, it's not ordinary.<br /><br />Just like other Dee's books, her words go through my mind and force themselves to my heart. Her way of writing forced me not only to feel it using my brain, but also my heart. :)<br /><br />Recommended if you're a forever in love person or love enthusiast. It'd make some love-pessimists cringe in disgust tho.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer1565728578104354067">Another masterpiece by Dee.<br/><br/>The concept was original, producing two ways to enjoy the fiction. Haven't actually bought the CD, but have listened to their tracks over from their website.<br/><br/>It's very 'Dee'. Firasat is my fave among all. Followed closely by Malaikat Juga Tahu. Friends who haven't followed Dee have tell me that this is kinda heavy and that they don't understand her way of thinking. It may not as light as Filsafat Kopi, but sure it's not as heavy as Supernova. </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer40720050" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14613892421359604705">Not as good as "Filosofi Kopi" but still distinctly clear, witty and just so Dee. As always, Dee unearths a profound meaning beneath a simple surface that's often taken for granted and is careful about rhythm, diction and grammar. She's a fluent storyteller, not even once falter in her step thus making all her stories in this book a lucid enjoyment to read. Regarding the so-Dee tone, I often have to remind myself that it's a story and not her lifestory itself.<br/><br/>Thumbs up, Dee!</span>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('d/dphzTPEsvjxQnRshL+uZC6xtqBOxvlVanw0IszjloeWTgqzw9XtolaIvBCGHlQUon7wDO8vA11aVEyhSn4eg==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('NKbIKSKB+W/Il14PhTjIXqzaTt7F1DMqqqDQ50L2DuRdCJmE2UG8EqIIdS51Mk+3bulzxHdTlMKKYHEFTOx4xA==')})
  }

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/164478.Dee_Lestari">About Dee Lestari</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>
<a href="/author/show/164478.Dee_Lestari"><div class='bookAuthorProfile__photo' style='background-image: url(https://images.gr-assets.com/authors/1185996159p3/164478.jpg);'></div>
</a></div>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__widgetContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__name'>
<a href="/author/show/164478.Dee_Lestari">Dee Lestari

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer5450432267194808588">Dee Lestari, is one of the bestselling and critically acclaimed writers in Indonesia.<br/>Born in January 20, 1976, she began her debut with a serial novel: Supernova in 2001. Supernova’s first episode, <i>Kesatria, Putri, dan Bintang Jatuh</i> (The Knight, The Princess, and The Falling Star), was sold phenomenally, achieving a cult status among Indonesian young readers. She has published four other episodes:</span>
  <span id="freeText5450432267194808588" style="display:none">Dee Lestari, is one of the bestselling and critically acclaimed writers in Indonesia.<br />Born in January 20, 1976, she began her debut with a serial novel: Supernova in 2001. Supernova’s first episode, <i>Kesatria, Putri, dan Bintang Jatuh</i> (The Knight, The Princess, and The Falling Star), was sold phenomenally, achieving a cult status among Indonesian young readers. She has published four other episodes: <i>Akar</i> (The Root), <i>Petir</i> (The Lightning), <i>Partikel</i>(The Particle), and <i>Gelombang</i> (The Wave). <br />Aside of the Supernova series, Dee has also published a novel titled <i>Perahu Kertas</i> (Paper Boat), and three anthologies: <i>Filosofi Kopi</i> (Coffee’s Philosophy), <i>Madre</i>, and <i>Rectoverso</i> — a unique hybrid of music and literature. <br />Dee also has an extensive music career, producing four albums with her former vocal trio, and two solo albums. She has been writing songs for renowned Indonesian artists. <br /><i>Perahu Kertas</i> (Paper Boat) was turned into a movie in 2009, marking Dee’s debut as a screenplay writer. The movie became one of the national's block busters. Following the same path, <i>Madre, Filosofi Kopi, Madre,</i> and <i>Supernova KPBJ,</i> were made into movies. <br />In February 2016, Dee released the final episode of Supernova, <i>Inteligensi Embun Pagi</i> (Intelligence of the Morning Dew). All Dee’s books are published by Bentang Pustaka. </span>
  <a data-text-id="5450432267194808588" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
</div>
